              At Vodafone, we believe that connectivity is a force for good. If we use it for the things that really matter, it can improve people's lives and the world around us.  
Through our technology we empower people, connecting everyone regardless of who they are or where they live, we protect the planet and help our customers do the same. 

But we’re not just shaping the future of technology for our customers – we’re shaping the future for everyone who joins our team too. When you work with us, you’re part of a global mission to connect people, solve complex challenges, and create a sustainable, more inclusive world. 
If you want to grow your career whilst finding the perfect balance between work and life, Vodafone offers the opportunities and support to help you belong and make a real impact.

#EveryoneConnected

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Working with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/ast-spacemobile?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>AST SpaceMobile</a>, we’re on a mission to bring customers the best network and to connect people without mobile access 🚀🌍 

Touring our partner’s Midland facilities, our CEO Margherita Della Valle and members of the Vodafone team were able to discuss how we accelerate bringing satellite mobile broadband deployment across Europe.

These discussions build on our satellite progress this year. From making the world’s first space-based mobile video call using standard smartphones in January, to launching our SatCo joint venture which will bring seamless direct-to-cell satellite connectivity to areas of little or no mobile coverage in Europe 📶📱 

Learn more about our partnership here: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dhjbbyX8?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dhjbbyX8</a>
 
<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fvodafone&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Vodafone</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fastspacemobile&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ASTSpaceMobile</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fdirecttocell&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#DirecttoCell</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fbroadband&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Broadband</a> </p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Last week we welcomed our new Graduates and Apprentices into Vodafone Group UK ❤️  Their first day was spent at Newbury HQ learning all about life at Vodafone and hearing from guest speakers, including some of our brilliant current grads and apprentices.

<a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/toby-jones03?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Toby Jones Assoc CIPD</a>, second year HR graduate, spent his latest rotation with the Early Careers team, which saw him take on the role of one of the key facilitators for the whole induction process:
"It was an absolute joy and priviledge to welcome our new Group Graduates and Apprentices at their induction. As a Group HR Graduate myself, it was an amazing opportunity to be able to organise and bring our new Early careers cohort into the world of Vodafone, helping them settle and feel a real sense of belonging, which is exactly how I have felt in my first year of being here."

Welcome to our new 2025 Early Careers Cohort - we can't wait to see you grow your careers and the inevitable impact you'll make with us 🤩 

Want to be a part of our 2026 cohort? Applications for our Graduate programmes are now open!         attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Subsea cables carry the vast majority of the world’s data traffic.

These underwater systems are vital to the digital economy – but who is safeguarding them for the future? What happens when a cable breaks?

We visited one of our Subsea Cable Stations in the UK to see the engineers and technicians, who keep the world connected, in action. 

Featuring major projects like <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2F2africa&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#2Africa</a> and the India-Europe-Xpress (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fiex&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IEX</a>), discover the evolution of subsea networks and their growing importance in meeting global digital demand.

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Subsea cables carry the vast majority of the world’s data traffic.

These underwater systems are vital to the digital economy – but who is safeguarding them for the future? What happens when a cable breaks?

We visited one of our Subsea Cable Stations in the UK to see the engineers and technicians, who keep the world connected, in action. 

Featuring major projects like <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2F2africa&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#2Africa</a> and the India-Europe-Xpress (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fiex&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IEX</a>), discover the evolution of subsea networks and their growing importance in meeting global digital demand.
